CREATE TABLE bookings (id INT PRIMARY KEY, trip_id INT REFERENCES trips(id), traveler_id INT REFERENCES travelers(id), booking_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (trip_id) REFERENCES trips(id), FOREIGN KEY (traveler_id) REFERENCES travelers(id))
